val_generator = val_gen.flow_from_directory(data_val_path, target_size, shuffle=False, batch_size=batch_size)
test_generator = test_gen.flow_from_directory(data_test_path, target_size, shuffle=False, batch_size=batch_size)

Build NN¶

In [14]:
from sklearn.metrics import confusion_matrix

from keras.utils.np_utils import to_categorical # convert to one-hot-encoding
from keras.models import Sequential, Model
from keras.layers import Dense, Dropout, Input, Flatten, Conv2D, MaxPooling2D, BatchNormalization, LSTM, Lambda, GlobalAveragePooling2D, Concatenate, ZeroPadding2D
from keras.optimizers import *
from keras.applications import *
In [15]:
%%time
input_tensor = Input((height, width, 3))
input_tensor_DN = Lambda(densenet.preprocess_input)(input_tensor)
input_tensor_XC = Lambda(xception.preprocess_input)(input_tensor)
input_tensor_IV3 = Lambda(inception_v3.preprocess_input)(input_tensor)
input_tensor_IRNV2 = Lambda(inception_resnet_v2.preprocess_input)(input_tensor)

base_model_DN201 = DenseNet201(input_tensor=input_tensor_DN, weights='imagenet', include_top=False)
base_model_XC = Xception(input_tensor=input_tensor_XC, weights='imagenet', include_top=False)
base_model_IV3 = InceptionV3(input_tensor=input_tensor_IV3, weights='imagenet', include_top=False)
base_model_IRNV2 = InceptionResNetV2(input_tensor=input_tensor_IRNV2, weights='imagenet', include_top=False)

concat = Concatenate(name='my_concat')([
    ZeroPadding2D(padding=((1, 0), (1, 0)), data_format=None)(base_model_DN201.output),
    base_model_XC.output, 
    ZeroPadding2D(padding=((1, 1), (1, 1)), data_format=None)(base_model_IV3.output), 
    ZeroPadding2D(padding=((1, 1), (1, 1)), data_format=None)(base_model_IRNV2.output)
])
conv = Conv2D(512, (1, 1), activation='relu', padding='same', name='my_conv')(concat)
gap = GlobalAveragePooling2D()(conv)

x = Dense(512, activation='relu')(gap)
x = Dense(128, activation='softmax')(x)

model = Model(inputs=input_tensor, outputs=x)

for layer in base_model_DN201.layers:
    layer.trainable = False
for layer in base_model_DN201.layers[642:]:
    layer.trainable = True
    
for layer in base_model_XC.layers:
    layer.trainable = False
# Last block: 116
for layer in base_model_XC.layers[116:]:
    layer.trainable = True
    
for layer in base_model_IV3.layers:
    layer.trainable = False
# Last block: 277
for layer in base_model_IV3.layers[277:]:
    layer.trainable = True
    
for layer in base_model_IRNV2.layers:
    layer.trainable = False
# Last block: 618
for layer in base_model_IRNV2.layers[618:]:
    layer.trainable = True

CPU times: user 1min 53s, sys: 0 ns, total: 1min 53s
Wall time: 1min 52s

def get_lr(x):
#     lr = round(3e-4 * 0.96 ** x, 6)
#     if lr < 1e-5:
#         lr = 1e-5
    
    if x <= 5:
        lr = 3e-4
    elif x > 5 and x <= 20:
        lr = 1e-4
    else:
        lr = 5e-5
    print(lr, end='  ')
    return lr

for i in range(30):
    print(get_lr(i), end=' ')
# annealer = LearningRateScheduler(lambda x: 1e-3 * 0.9 ** x)
annealer = LearningRateScheduler(get_lr)

early_stop = EarlyStopping(monitor='acc', min_delta=0.01, patience=0.005, verbose=0, mode='auto')

log_dir = os.path.join(log_folder, run_name)
print('\nlog_dir: %s' % log_dir)
tensorBoard = TensorBoard(log_dir=log_dir)


callbacks = []
callbacks = [tensorBoard, annealer, early_stop]

In [28]:
def save_network(model, run_name):
    cwd = os.getcwd()
    modelPath = os.path.join(cwd, 'model')
    if not os.path.isdir(modelPath):
        os.mkdir(modelPath)
    weigthsFile = os.path.join(modelPath, run_name + '.h5')
    model.save(weigthsFile)
save_network(model, run_name_acc)

def save_network(model, run_name):
    cwd = os.getcwd()
    modelPath = os.path.join(cwd, 'model')
    if not os.path.isdir(modelPath):
        os.mkdir(modelPath)
    weigthsFile = os.path.join(modelPath, run_name + '.h5')
    model.save(weigthsFile)
save_network(model, run_name_acc)

%%time
max_indexes = np.argmax(y_pred, -1)
print(max_indexes.shape)

test_dict = {}
for pair in zip(test_generator.filenames, max_indexes):
    image_name, indx = pair[0], int(pair[1])
    image_name = image_name.split('/')[-1]
    image_id = int(image_name.split('.')[0])
#     print(pair[0], image_name, image_id, indx, indx+1, type(image_id), type(indx))
    test_dict[image_id] = indx + 1

#确认图片的id是否能与ImageDataGenerator()对应上
for name in test_generator.filenames[:10]:

    image_id = int(image_name.split('.')[0])

In [42]:
%%time
len_sample_submission_csv = len(sample_submission_csv)
print('len(len_sample_submission_csv)=%d' % len_sample_submission_csv)
count = 0
for i in range(len_sample_submission_csv):
    image_id = int(sample_submission_csv.iloc[i, 0])
    if image_id in test_dict:
        pred_label = test_dict[image_id]
#         print('%s\t%s' % (image_id, pred_label))
        sample_submission_csv.iloc[i, 1] = pred_label
    else:
#         print('%s\t%s' % (image_id, 20))
        sample_submission_csv.iloc[i, 1] = 20 # 属于20的类最多，所以全都设置成这个类，可能会比设置成其他得到的结果好
    count += 1
    if count % 1000 == 0:
        print(int(count/1000), end=' ')
display(sample_submission_csv.head(2))
